- 2207 Undenatured ethyl alcohol with an alcoholic strength by volume of 80% vol. or more; ethyl alcohol and other spirits denatured, with any alcohol content,
- 2208 Undenatured ethyl alcohol with an alcoholic strength by volume of less than 80% vol; spirits, liqueurs and other spirituous beverages;
- 2401 Unprocessed tobacco; tobacco waste,
- 2402 Cigars (whether or not cut off), cigarillos (cigarillos) and cigarettes from tobacco or tobacco substitutes,
- 2403 Other tobacco products and tobacco substitutes; homogenised or reconstituted tobacco; tobacco extracts and punishments (essences),
- 8525 20 91 Transmitting devices containing reception devices: For a cellular network (mobile phones),
- 8525 20 99 Transmitting apparatus containing the receiving equipment: Other,
- 8529 90 40 Parts suitable for use solely or principally with apparatus of headings 8525 to 8528.
Other: Parts of apparatus falling within subheadings 8525 10 50, 8525 20 91, 8525 20 99, 8525 40 11 and 8527 90 92.
JCD entries from the customs databases of the Czech Republic and Slovakia were assigned to each other on the basis of the agreement of individual JCD paragraphs (e.g. invoiced price, quantity, weight, registration plate of the vehicle carrying cargo, date of crossing the national border, customs tariff item, etc.).
The results of the comparison are presented in the following tables and charts.
The mutual allocation of individual imports and exports was made more difficult, among other things, by the fact that commercial transactions were not declared in the same way on both sides.
For example, exports from the Czech Republic declared on one export JCD were declared on several import JCDs in the territory of the Slovak Republic, or the export JCD had a different number of items from the import JCD.
Other factors that influenced the success of the assignment were the different composition of the data in the customs databases of the Czech Republic and Slovakia, as well as the time shift between the export records in the customs database of one country and the registration of corresponding imports in the customs database of the other country.
The results of the comparison were used in the selection of control samples at the financial or tax authorities audited.
Priority was chosen for some tax entities that made imports or exports between the Czech Republic and Slovakia, which could not be identified in both databases.
Furthermore, some tax entities were selected for the verification of business transactions reported in VAT returns, for which data on imports or exports between the Czech Republic and Slovakia were found in both databases.
4.3. Pilot control at the border customs crossing of Starý Hrozenkov-Drietoma
The border customs crossing for the performance of pilot control was selected on the basis of a joint analysis of the unassigned JCD items in the customs databases of the Czech Republic and Slovakia.
On the basis of a bilateral agreement between the customs authorities of the Czech Republic and the Slovak Republic, the use of control sheets has been introduced at border customs crossings between the Czech Republic and Slovakia since 1.6.1998.
The aim of this measure was to eliminate customs and tax evasion as far as possible, to ensure an overview of the movement of means of transport carrying goods of a commercial nature in the customs area and to create the conditions for mutual comparison of customs records.
The joint pilot inspection was carried out on 8.3.2004 to 26.3.2004 and was aimed at examining this customs control system.
Procedure for the use of control certificates at the Starý Hrozenkov-Drietoma border crossing:
1) Consideration of the vehicle, issue of the inspection sheet and hand it over to the driver.
2) Shutdown of the vehicle in the designated sector in the parking lot.
Customs discussions in the check-in hall check-in hall of the Police of the Czech Republic, Police of the Slovak Republic, Customs Administration of the Czech Republic, Customs Administration of the Slovak Republic.
The execution of the check-in was confirmed by the individual components with a stamp on the checklist.
3) Landing a vehicle into the area of carrying out a physical check.
Presentation of the inspection sheet, JCD, or other documents to the customs officer - check the execution of all prescribed operations and documents.
Performance of physical inspection by the relevant files.
Removal of the vehicle from the customs area.
Pozru: When goods were imported into the Czech Republic, the weighing of the vehicles were carried out directly by the staff of the Customs Administration of the Czech Republic.
When goods were imported into the SR, weighing vehicles were carried out by staff of a designated legal entity.
The vehicles were registered in computer records after consideration.

Within the framework of international cooperation, the implementation of imports and exports between the Czech Republic and Slovakia was verified from the documents of customs administrations and financial and tax authorities on the territory of the other state.
Selected tax entities have been verified:
- whether the submitted JCD was registered in the customs databases of the Czech Republic and Slovakia,
- fulfilment of the legal conditions for the application of the VAT deduction on importation, the refund of excess VAT deduction and the application of the VAT exemption on export.
The verification of commercial transactions was found to be:

VAT was paid to the competent customs office in the SR.

In the SR customs database it was not possible to identify the corresponding import JCD to 4 export JCD (9 items) with a total statistical value of 399 776 CZK.
The competent tax authority in the Slovak Republic verified these imports from the taxpayer.
The tax entity, listed on the JCD as an importer in the Slovak Republic, commented in the minutes of the local investigation that it had not implemented the imports declared on Czech export JCDs.
The SAO of SR therefore asked the local competent tax authority to carry out a tax audit of VAT and corporate income tax for the 2002 and 2003 tax.

In the VAT tax returns, the company did not report any exports in 2002 and 2003.
